		<h1 class="title">How to Make Homemade Caramel</h1>
		<div class="long-post" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage"><p>We&#8217;re breaking down exactly <strong>how to make homemade caramel</strong>. Rich and delicious, this easy caramel sauce is perfect for all sorts of recipes! Use it as a filling in a salted caramel cake, drizzle it over ice cream, or just eat the best caramel sauce by the spoonful! We took out any guess work out of this caramel recipe with step by step photos so you&#8217;ll know exactly how to make caramel with nothing left to second guess!</p>
<p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23275" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%202400%203600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="easy homemade caramel in a glass jar with a drip" width="2400" height="3600" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-5.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23275" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-5.jpg" alt="easy homemade caramel in a glass jar with a drip" width="2400" height="3600" /></noscript></p>
<h2 style="text-align: center;">How to Make Homemade Caramel</h2>
<p>Happy hump day! This week is flying by for us, so let&#8217;s take a moment to stop and smell the roses&#8230;or stop and eat the salted caramel 🙂 Today we&#8217;re sharing our foolproof recipe for the best homemade caramel you&#8217;ll ever have. Made with just three easy ingredients and no special equipment or thermometers, we&#8217;re here to show you that homemade caramel sauce is actually super approachable.</p>
<p><span id="more-23351"></span></p>
<p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23276" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%202400%203600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="spoonful of easy homemade caramel on parchment paper" width="2400" height="3600" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6.jpg 2400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 2400px) 100vw, 2400px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23276" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6.jpg" alt="spoonful of easy homemade caramel on parchment paper" width="2400" height="3600" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6.jpg 2400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-6-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 2400px) 100vw, 2400px" /></noscript></p>
<h2>Our tips for the best homemade caramel:</h2>
<ol>
<li><strong>Use high quality butter: </strong>You’re only as good as your ingredients and with caramel your butter quality can really make or break your sauce. This is one time when it’s a good idea to splurge on that box that’s a few dollars more expensive.</li>
<li><strong>Never leave your caramel sauce unattended: </strong>To make caramel sauce you essentially toast white sugar until it’s melted, before adding in butter, cream, and salt. Your sugar can go from toasty to burnt pretty quickly though, so make sure you keep a close eye on it!</li>
<li><strong>Don’t forget the salt! </strong>Caramel is simply too sweet without it. A healthy amount of salt really deepens the flavor profile and will keep your caramel from tasting overly sweet.</li>
</ol>
<p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23279" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%202400%203600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="salted caramel dripping into jar off of spoon" width="2400" height="3600" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3.jpg 2400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 2400px) 100vw, 2400px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23279" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3.jpg" alt="salted caramel dripping into jar off of spoon" width="2400" height="3600" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3.jpg 2400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-3-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 2400px) 100vw, 2400px" /></noscript></p>
<p>This step by step guide will break it allllll down for you so that you, too, can eat delicious salted caramel by the spoonful unashamedly in your home. YOU. ARE. WELCOME.</p>
<p>Let&#8217;s get to it, babes.</p>
<p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23277" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%202400%203600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="easy homemade caramel in a glass jar" width="2400" height="3600" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4.jpg 2400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 2400px) 100vw, 2400px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23277" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4.jpg" alt="easy homemade caramel in a glass jar" width="2400" height="3600" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4.jpg 2400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-4-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 2400px) 100vw, 2400px" /></noscript></p>
<h3>Step One: Place the sugar in a heavy bottomed saucepan over medium heat</h3>
<h4>Move the sauce pan around every few minutes to keep the sugar heating evenly, but do NOT stir constantly</h4>
<p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23274" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%202400%203600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="homemade caramel stage one sugar begins to clump" width="2400" height="3600" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots.jpg 2400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 2400px) 100vw, 2400px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23274" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots.jpg" alt="homemade caramel stage one sugar begins to clump" width="2400" height="3600" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots.jpg 2400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 2400px) 100vw, 2400px" /></noscript></p>
<p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23273" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%202400%203600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="homemade caramel sugar started data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-2.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23273" <h3>Step Two: Keep an eye on the sugar, stirring it every few minutes until it melts.</h3>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23272 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="homemade caramel process shot sugar half melted" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23272 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-1067x1600.jpg" alt="homemade caramel process shot sugar half melted" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-3-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" /></noscript></p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23271 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Sugar is melted with a few clumps remaining" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23271 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-1067x1600.jpg" alt="Sugar is melted with a few clumps remaining" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-4-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" /></noscript></p>
<p>The sugar will clump first and eventually start to melt. This can take up to 15 minutes. Be patient! You&#8217;ll know your caramel is done when it&#8217;s fully liquid and no clumps of sugar remain.</p>
<p><strong>This is what your caramel should look like by the end of this step:</strong></p>
<p><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23270" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%202400%203600'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="sugar is completley smooth and no clumps remain" width="2400" height="3600" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-5.jpg 2400w, data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-5.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone size-full wp-image-23270" <h3>Step Three: Remove from heat. Add butter to the melted sugar and stir to combine.</h3>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23269 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="butter being stirred into easy homemade caramel sauce" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-6-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-6-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-6-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-6-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-6-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23269 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-6-1067x1600.jpg" alt="butter being stirred into easy homemade caramel sauce" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-7-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-7-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23268 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-7-1067x1600.jpg" alt="whisking butter into caramel sauce" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-7-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-7-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-7-400x600.jpg 400w, <p>The mixture will begin to bubble violently.</p>
<p>Now, I know the normal human reaction to this would be alarm, but this is exactly what the homemade caramel should be doing! The butter is much colder in comparison to the hot sugar, so they&#8217;re just trying to get to know each other. Sparks are flying.</p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23267 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="butter being stirred into easy homemade caramel sauce" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23267 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-1067x1600.jpg" alt="butter being stirred into easy homemade caramel sauce" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-8-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" /></noscript></p>
<p>After a few minutes of stirring the two will start to combine. Just keep whisking until they are completely homogenous</p>
<p><strong>This is what the caramel should look like by the end of this step:</strong></p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23266 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="butter and sugar are combined" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23266 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-1067x1600.jpg" alt="butter and sugar are combined" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-9-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" /></noscript></p>
<h3>Step Four: Pour in the cream and salt, and stir until completely combined.</h3>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23265 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="cream poured into saucepan with caramel" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23265 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-1067x1600.jpg" alt="cream poured into saucepan with caramel" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-10-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" /></noscript></p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23263 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="cream full incorporated into salted caramel" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23263 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-1067x1600.jpg" alt="cream full incorporated into salted caramel" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-Process-Shots-12-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" /></noscript></p>
<p><strong>This is what the caramel will look like at the end!</strong></p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23280 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="salted caramel dripping off spoon in to a jar" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23280 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-1067x1600.jpg" alt="salted caramel dripping off spoon in to a jar" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-2-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" /></noscript></p>
<h2>What recipes to use homemade caramel sauce in?</h2>
<p>I could go on for literally forever. Caramel pretty much goes with everything in my opinion, but here are a few of our favs:</p>
<ul>
<li>drizzled over <a href="https://bromabakery.com/pumpkin-cake-with-cream-cheese-frosting/">pumpkin cake</a></li>
<li>in a <a href="https://bromabakery.com/hazelnut-salted-caramel-chocolate-tarts/">hazelnut salted caramel tar</a>t</li>
<li>as the filling in a cake</li>
<li>in homemade candy bars</li>
<li>sandwiched together between <a href="https://bromabakery.com/chai-spiced-salted-caramel-macarons-recipe/">chai macarons</a>,</li>
<li>poured over ice cream</li>
<li>in <a href="https://bromabakery.com/sweet-potato-cupcakes-with-cream-cheese-frosting-and-caramel-drizzle/">salted caramel sweet potato cupcakes</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Or&#8230;just by the spoonful. We won&#8217;t judge 🙂</p>
<p><img class="alignnone wp-image-23278 size-large" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%20viewBox='0%200%20780%201170'%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="homemade caramel falling off of spoon into jar" width="780" height="1170" data-lazy-srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-195x293.jpg 195w" data-lazy-sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" data-lazy-src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-1067x1600.jpg" /><noscript><img class="alignnone wp-image-23278 size-large" src="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-1067x1600.jpg" alt="homemade caramel falling off of spoon into jar" width="780" height="1170" srcset="https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-1067x1600.jpg 1067w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-100x150.jpg 100w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-400x600.jpg 400w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-300x450.jpg 300w, https://bromabakery.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/10/Easy-Homemade-Caramel-195x293.jpg 195w" sizes="(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px" /></noscript></p>
<h2>How to store this easy caramel sauce:</h2>
<p>You can store this caramel sauce in an air tight container (we love mason jars!) in the fridge for 1 month or freeze for up to 3 months!</p>
<p>Now that you know exactly how to make homemade caramel, no more excuses, guys. It is  soooo much better than any kind you could buy at the store. Happy caramel eating 🙂</p>

<div class="mobile-stuff">

		<h3>Ingredients</h3>
		<ul>
<li><span class="nutrifox-quantity" data-nf-original="usc" data-nf-usc="1" data-nf-metric="200" data-unit="cup" data-nf-usc-unit="cup" data-nf-metric-unit="gram" data-nf-food-id="6319" data-nf-food-description="Sugars, granulated" data-amount="1">1</span> <span class="nutrifox-unit" data-nf-original="usc" data-nf-usc="cup" data-nf-metric="gram" data-nf-food-id="6319" data-nf-food-description="Sugars, granulated">cup</span> sugar</li>
<li><span data-amount="6" data-unit="tablespoon">6 tablespoons</span> unsalted butter, room temperature</li>
<li><span class="nutrifox-quantity" data-nf-original="usc" data-nf-usc="0.5" data-nf-metric="118.5" data-unit="cup" data-nf-usc-unit="cup" data-nf-metric-unit="ml" data-nf-food-id="52" data-nf-food-description="Cream, fluid, heavy whipping" data-amount="0.5">1/2</span> <span class="nutrifox-unit" data-nf-original="usc" data-nf-usc="cup" data-nf-metric="ml" data-nf-food-id="52" data-nf-food-description="Cream, fluid, heavy whipping">cup</span> cream</li>
<li><span data-amount="0.5">1/2</span> to <span data-amount="1">1</span> teaspoon sea salt</li>
</ul>
	</div>
		
		
			<div class="tasty-recipes-instructions">
			<h3>Instructions</h3>
			<ol>
<li id="instruction-step-1">In a heavy bottomed sauce pan, heat the sugar on medium low heat until its completely melted, swirling the pan gently every 20 seconds or so. The sugar will start to form clumps before melting slowly. Be patient and keep an eye on it to make sure it does not burn.</li>
<li id="instruction-step-2">Once melted, remove from heat immediately and stir in the butter. The mixture will violently bubble. You’re doing it right.</li>
<li id="instruction-step-3">Next, pour in the heavy cream and 1/2 teaspoon of the sea salt. Stir until everything is combined. Taste a spoonful of cooled caramel. If desired add the remaining sea salt to taste!</li>
<li id="instruction-step-4">Pour into small bowl or cup and allow to cool completely before using.*</li>
</ol>

			<h3>Notes</h3>
			<ul>
<li>Make sure you use a high quality butter! Caramel is made from so few ingredients that the butter and cream&#8217;s quality really shines through!</li>
<li>For thicker caramel, only add 1/3 cup of cream!</li>
<li>Feel free to add any additions you like at the the end. We love to add a teaspoon of vanilla extract, cinnamon, ginger&#8230;the options are endless!</li>
<li>Caramel can be stored in an air tight container in the fridge for 1 month or in the freezer for 3 months!</li>
</ul>

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript" style="display: none !important;">
(function(){
	/* frac.js (C) 2012-present SheetJS -- http://sheetjs.com */
	/* bothEquals() avoids use of &&, which gets prettified by WordPress. */
	var bothEquals = function( d1, d2, D ) {
		var ret = 0;
		if (d1<=D) {
			ret++;
		}
		if (d2<=D) {
			ret++;
		}
		return ret === 2;
	};
	var frac =function frac(x,D,mixed){var n1=Math.floor(x),d1=1;var n2=n1+1,d2=1;if(x!==n1)while(bothEquals(d1,d2,D)){var m=(n1+n2)/(d1+d2);if(x===m){if(d1+d2<=D){d1+=d2;n1+=n2;d2=D+1}else if(d1>d2)d2=D+1;else d1=D+1;break}else if(x<m){n2=n1+n2;d2=d1+d2}else{n1=n1+n2;d1=d1+d2}}if(d1>D){d1=d2;n1=n2}if(!mixed)return[0,n1,d1];var q=Math.floor(n1/d1);return[q,n1-q*d1,d1]};frac.cont=function cont(x,D,mixed){var sgn=x<0?-1:1;var B=x*sgn;var P_2=0,P_1=1,P=0;var Q_2=1,Q_1=0,Q=0;var A=Math.floor(B);while(Q_1<D){A=Math.floor(B);P=A*P_1+P_2;Q=A*Q_1+Q_2;if(B-A<5e-8)break;B=1/(B-A);P_2=P_1;P_1=P;Q_2=Q_1;Q_1=Q}if(Q>D){if(Q_1>D){Q=Q_2;P=P_2}else{Q=Q_1;P=P_1}}if(!mixed)return[0,sgn*P,Q];var q=Math.floor(sgn*P/Q);return[q,sgn*P-q*Q,Q]};

	/* {'¼': '1/4','½': '1/2','¾': '3/4','⅓': '1/3','⅔':'2/3','⅕':'1/5','⅖':'2/5','⅗':'3/5','⅘':'4/5','⅙':'1/6','⅚':'5/6','⅛':'1/8','⅜':'3/8','⅝':'5/8','⅞':'7/8'} */
	window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions = JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent("%7B%22%C2%BC%22%3A%221%2F4%22%2C%22%C2%BD%22%3A%221%2F2%22%2C%22%C2%BE%22%3A%223%2F4%22%2C%22%E2%85%93%22%3A%221%2F3%22%2C%22%E2%85%94%22%3A%222%2F3%22%2C%22%E2%85%95%22%3A%221%2F5%22%2C%22%E2%85%96%22%3A%222%2F5%22%2C%22%E2%85%97%22%3A%223%2F5%22%2C%22%E2%85%98%22%3A%224%2F5%22%2C%22%E2%85%99%22%3A%221%2F6%22%2C%22%E2%85%9A%22%3A%225%2F6%22%2C%22%E2%85%9B%22%3A%221%2F8%22%2C%22%E2%85%9C%22%3A%223%2F8%22%2C%22%E2%85%9D%22%3A%225%2F8%22%2C%22%E2%85%9E%22%3A%227%2F8%22%7D"));

	window.tastyRecipesFormatAmount = function(amount, el) {
		if ( parseFloat( amount ) === parseInt( amount ) ) {
			return amount;
		}
		var roundType = 'frac';
		if (typeof el.dataset.amountShouldRound !== 'undefined') {
			if ('false' != el.dataset.amountShouldRound) {
				if ( 'number' === el.dataset.amountShouldRound ) {
					roundType = 'number';
				} else if ('frac' === el.dataset.amountShouldRound) {
					roundType = 'frac'
				} else if ('vulgar' === el.dataset.amountShouldRound) {
					roundType = 'vulgar'
				} else {
					roundType = 'integer';
				}
			}
		}
		if ('number' === roundType) {
			amount = Number.parseFloat(amount).toPrecision(2);
		} else if ('integer' === roundType) {
			amount = Math.round(amount);
		} else if ('frac' === roundType || 'vulgar' === roundType) {
			var denom = 8;
			if (typeof el.dataset.unit !== 'undefined') {
				var unit = el.dataset.unit;
				if (['cups','cup','c'].includes(unit)) {
					denom = 4;
					if (0.125 === amount) {
						denom = 8;
					}
					if ("0.1667" === Number.parseFloat( amount ).toPrecision(4)) {
						denom = 6;
					}
				}
				if (['tablespoons','tablespoon','tbsp'].includes(unit)) {
					denom = 2;
				}
				if (['teaspoons','teaspoon','tsp'].includes(unit)) {
					denom = 8;
				}
			}
			var amountArray = frac.cont( amount, denom, true );
			var newAmount = '';
			if ( amountArray[1] !== 0 ) {
				newAmount = amountArray[1] + '/' + amountArray[2];
				if ('vulgar' === roundType) {
					Object.keys(window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions).forEach(function(vulgar) {
						if (newAmount === window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions[vulgar]) {
							newAmount = vulgar;
						}
					});
				}
			}
			if ( newAmount ) {
				newAmount = ' ' + newAmount;
			}
			if ( amountArray[0] ) {
				newAmount = amountArray[0] + newAmount;
			}
			amount = newAmount;
		}
		return amount;
	}
}())

</script>
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript" style="display: none !important;">
(function(){
	var buttonClass = 'tasty-recipes-convert-button',
		buttonActiveClass = 'tasty-recipes-convert-button-active',
		buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.tasty-recipes-convert-button');
	if ( ! buttons ) {
		return;
	}
	buttons.forEach(function(button){
		button.addEventListener('click', function(event){
			event.preventDefault();
			var recipe = event.target.closest('.tasty-recipes');
			if ( ! recipe ) {
				return;
			}
			var otherButtons = recipe.querySelectorAll('.' + buttonClass);
			otherButtons.forEach(function(bt){
				bt.classList.remove(buttonActiveClass);
			});
			button.classList.add(buttonActiveClass);
			var unitType = button.dataset.unitType;
			var dataset = 'nf' + unitType.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + unitType.slice(1);
			var convertables = recipe.querySelectorAll('span[data-nf-original]');
			convertables.forEach(function(convertable){
				if (typeof convertable.dataset.amountOriginalType === 'undefined'
					&& 'usc' === convertable.dataset.nfOriginal) {
					if (-1 !== convertable.innerText.indexOf('/')) {
						convertable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'frac';
					}
					if (-1 !== convertable.innerText.indexOf('.')) {
						convertable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'number';
					}
					Object.keys(window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions).forEach(function(vulgar) {
						if (-1 !== convertable.innerText.indexOf(vulgar)) {
							convertable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'vulgar';
						}
					})
				}
				convertable.innerText = convertable.dataset[dataset];
				if (typeof convertable.dataset.unit !== 'undefined') {
					convertable.dataset.unit = convertable.dataset[dataset + 'Unit'];
				}
				if (typeof convertable.dataset.amount !== 'undefined') {
					convertable.dataset.amount = convertable.dataset[dataset];
					if ('metric' === unitType) {
						convertable.dataset.amountShouldRound = parseInt(convertable.dataset.amount) >= 10 ? 'integer' : 'number';
					} else if (typeof convertable.dataset.amountOriginalType !== 'undefined') {
						convertable.dataset.amountShouldRound = convertable.dataset.amountOriginalType;
					} else {
						convertable.dataset.amountShouldRound = false;
					}
					convertable.innerText = window.tastyRecipesFormatAmount(convertable.dataset[dataset], convertable);
				}
				if (convertable.classList.contains('nutrifox-unit')) {
					if ('gram' === convertable.dataset[dataset]) {
						convertable.innerText = 'grams';
					}
				}
			});
			/* Trigger the correct amount if scaling is active */
			document.querySelectorAll('.tasty-recipes-scale-button-active').forEach(function(scaleButton){
				scaleButton.click();
			});
		});
	});
}())

</script>
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript" style="display: none !important;">
(function(){
	var buttonClass = 'tasty-recipes-scale-button',
		buttonActiveClass = 'tasty-recipes-scale-button-active',
		buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.tasty-recipes-scale-button');
	if ( ! buttons ) {
		return;
	}

	buttons.forEach(function(button){
		button.addEventListener('click', function(event){
			event.preventDefault();
			var recipe = event.target.closest('.tasty-recipes');
			if ( ! recipe ) {
				return;
			}
			var otherButtons = recipe.querySelectorAll('.' + buttonClass);
			otherButtons.forEach(function(bt){
				bt.classList.remove(buttonActiveClass);
			});
			button.classList.add(buttonActiveClass);

			/* Scales all scalable amounts. */
			var scalables = recipe.querySelectorAll('span[data-amount]');
			var buttonAmount = parseFloat( button.dataset.amount );
			scalables.forEach(function(scalable){
				if (typeof scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType === 'undefined'
					&& typeof scalable.dataset.nfOriginal === 'undefined') {
					if (-1 !== scalable.innerText.indexOf('/')) {
						scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'frac';
					}
					if (-1 !== scalable.innerText.indexOf('.')) {
						scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'number';
					}
					Object.keys(window.tastyRecipesVulgarFractions).forEach(function(vulgar) {
						if (-1 !== scalable.innerText.indexOf(vulgar)) {
							scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType = 'vulgar';
						}
					})
					if (typeof scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType !== 'undefined') {
						scalable.dataset.amountShouldRound = scalable.dataset.amountOriginalType;
					}
				}
				var amount = parseFloat( scalable.dataset.amount ) * buttonAmount;
				amount = window.tastyRecipesFormatAmount(amount, scalable);
				if ( typeof scalable.dataset.unit !== 'undefined' ) {
					if ( ! scalable.classList.contains('nutrifox-quantity') ) {
						if ( ! scalable.classList.contains('nutrifox-second-quantity') ) {
							amount += ' ' + scalable.dataset.unit;
						}
					}
				}
				scalable.innerText = amount;
			});
			/* Appends " (x2)" indicator. */
			var nonNumerics = recipe.querySelectorAll('[data-has-non-numeric-amount]');
			nonNumerics.forEach(function(nonNumeric){
				var indicator = nonNumeric.querySelector('span[data-non-numeric-label]');
				if ( indicator ) {
					nonNumeric.removeChild(indicator);
				}
				if ( 1 !== buttonAmount ) {
					var indicator = document.createElement('span');
					indicator.setAttribute('data-non-numeric-label', true);
					var text = document.createTextNode(' (x' + buttonAmount + ')');
					indicator.appendChild(text);
					nonNumeric.appendChild(indicator);
				}
			});
		});
	});
}());

</script></div>
